Fujian Province Restores Local Education Fund Custody Committees in Each County 241

The local education funds of Fujian Province are managed by the Education Fund Custody Committees organized by each county. The nature of these committees is independent, and their funds are not mixed with other county funds. During the era of the 19th Route Army's administration last year, the provincial government passed a resolution to abolish the establishment of departments within the county education bureaus and reorganize the Local Property Custody Committees in each county, merging them with the Education Fund Custody Committees. Since the implementation of this policy, the county education funds have frequently been misappropriated. The current Director of Education, Zheng Zhenwen, deeply feels that educational administration and educational funding must be independent. Therefore, after proposing to the provincial government the restoration of the county education bureaus, he also proposed on the 4th of this month the restoration of the County Education Fund Custody Committee, which was passed by the meeting. The Department of Education issued a circular to all counties to promptly establish these committees. Regarding the Provincial Education Fund, the central government had suspended its allocation during the Fujian Incident. Upon resuming his position, Zheng Zhenwen strongly appealed to the central government, requesting that it continue to allocate 110,000 yuan per month from the national treasury until the consolidated tax system was reorganized, which was approved by the Ministry. Recently, due to the budget deficit in Fujian Province, the administrative expenses of various agencies were reduced to 75% of the previous year's budget, and the salaries of civil servants were discounted accordingly starting this month. However, the education sector receives full salaries without being affected by this. Moreover, salaries are paid around the 25th of each month, ensuring the stability of the lives of those in the education sector.

Promulgation of Order by the Anhui Education Department: Outline for New Life Training of Middle School Students 242

Anhui Provincial Government Education Department Director Yang Lian issued an order stating: The purpose of education lies in training the body and mind of young people and cultivating healthy citizens. It is closely related to the improvement of national morality and the improvement of social customs. At present, the effect of education in our country is not obvious. The reasons are not simple. The neglect of moral education in schools is the main reason. Therefore, in recent years, the central government has repeatedly issued clear orders to rectify the atmosphere of study. The department has also repeatedly ordered schools to pay attention to cultivating students' habits of cleanliness and orderliness, and to train them in the spirit of diligence and hard work. It also held a clean-up movement competition among various educational institutions in the provincial capital to supervise the implementation of various matters. Recently, Chairman Chiang Kai-shek launched the New Life Movement at the Nanchang camp. The main purpose is to cultivate frugality, diligence, cleanliness, hygiene, and a life in accordance with propriety, righteousness, integrity, and a sense of shame in the "clothing, food, housing, and transportation" of the people, thereby promoting the inherent spirit of the nation, and promoting the new opportunity to revive the nation. The news has spread, and the whole country has followed suit. It is good because our country's social economy is declining, and there is no way to save it without frugality; the national situation is weak, and there is no way to recover it without diligence; the people's physical fitness is weak, and there is no way to strengthen it without cleanliness and hygiene; the people's morality is declining, and there is no way to improve it without paying attention to propriety, righteousness, integrity, and a sense of shame. All these points are the necessary goals established to address the accumulated malpractices of the past. This kind of movement is the most necessary work to rejuvenate the country and revive the nation at present. Middle schools in this province should earnestly promote it. All school teachers and staff should take this as their goal for personal practice, and school moral education should take this as the standard for training students, so as to cultivate citizens with noble morals, sound knowledge and abilities, and become a model for society. Now, according to the main points of the New Life Movement in the Chairman's speech, the outline for the new life training of middle school students in this province is formulated and promulgated with the order. It is expected that the principals will follow the items listed, lead by example, practice diligently, supervise all the teachers and students of the school, practice hard day and night, and submit the situation of the preparation of the guiding order to the department for record within ten days after the document arrives. The department will send personnel to inspect the results at any time, distinguish the most important ones, and determine rewards and punishments. Do not violate or make mistakes. This order, the Outline for New Life Training of Middle School Students in Anhui Province.

1. General Outline and Training Objectives

Article 1: The Anhui Provincial Department of Education formulates this outline in order to rigorously implement the New Life Training for middle school students. Article 2: The New Life Training for middle schools aims to cultivate the following eight virtues and good habits in students: 1. Patriotism and public spirit: Should achieve the following items: Clothing, food, housing, and daily necessities should all use domestic goods, and absolutely not buy enemy goods. Should recognize national humiliation and national difficulties as the humiliation of the people, and always have the ambition to wipe out humiliation and save the country. Should earnestly participate in military training or scout training, and learn pure military skills. On the anniversary of national humiliation, one should reflect on whether one's own work is done diligently. One should resolutely abandon selfishness and self-interest and embrace the ambition to work for the country, society, and groups. One should respect the national flag and the flag of the Chinese Kuomintang. One should cherish public property. One should pay attention to public health. One should be enthusiastic about public undertakings. Others. 2. Frugality and simplicity: Should achieve the following items: Clothing, food, housing, and daily necessities should be simple and plain as much as possible, reduce unnecessary consumption and entertainment, absolutely do not smoke, absolutely do not drink, absolutely do not visit prostitutes or gamble, others. 3. Diligence and hard work: Should achieve the following items: Work should be started and finished quickly, work for the day should be completed, spare time should be used to do useful work, personal books and things should be tidied up diligently, dormitories and self-study rooms should be tidied up and cleaned diligently, one's own things should be done by oneself, do not instruct workers, cultivate labor skills, the spirit of hard work, hone the physique for resisting insults and fighting, and at least learn a proper life skill, be fearless of difficulties and not be content with ease, and have the spirit of sacrifice and struggle, others. 4. Cleanliness and hygiene: Should achieve the following items: The face should be washed clean, the hands should be washed clean, rinse the mouth and brush the teeth after eating, the hair should be combed and washed often, take a bath often, cut the nails often, button the buttons, wear the hat straight, the clothes should be neat, the bedding should be exposed to the sun and washed often, do not eat snacks, do not spit anywhere, do not eat unclean things, do not drink unboiled water, open the windows often, kill mosquitoes and flies, do not throw waste paper and rubbish everywhere, must throw them into the waste paper basket, get vaccinated for disease prevention, should have extracurricular sports, and at least have one sports skill, others. 5. Prudence and courtesy: Should achieve the following items: Stand up when singing the Party and national anthem, salute the teachers, students greet each other and salute each other, wait for others to finish speaking before speaking, do not make noises while drinking or chewing, do not curse people, do not hit people, reason in everything and do not quarrel, the voice of conversation should be small and the voice of speech should be loud, the attitude of speaking should be kind and do not rush to walk, say "sorry" when accidentally bumping into someone while walking, take off the hat when entering the house, do not wear a hat in the lecture hall or meeting place, say "good morning" when meeting in the morning, say "goodbye" when parting, do not shout loudly when walking, do not eat things, should cultivate the habit of prudence in dealing with things, should have the ability to use thinking to solve problems, others. 6. Friendship and mutual assistance: Should achieve the following items: Respect teachers, be filial to parents, love brothers and sisters, love classmates, help classmates, persuade people when they fight, help people who fall, help women, children, the elderly and provide services for them, have a spirit of cooperation, others. 7. Loyalty and sincerity: Should achieve the following items: Be realistic in doing things, be honest with people, be loyal to friends, be sincere, return what you find to the original owner, do not lie, admit your mistakes, correct your mistakes, do not blame others, do not accept what you should not accept, cultivate the habit of self-respect, others. 8. Obey the rules: Should achieve the following items: Abide by school rules, obey the guidance of training personnel, get up on time, sleep on time, work on time, wear uniforms, be punctual for appointments, be quiet in meetings, walk on the left side, enter and exit public places one by one in order, daily life should be regular and orderly, should wear the logo of the New Life Movement, after morning exercises or recess exercises, the whole body should sing the New Life Movement song together, others.

2. Training Personnel and Their Tasks

Article 3: The New Life Training of students in middle schools shall be presided over by the principal, and the director of teaching or the director of moral education and all teachers and staff shall assist. Article 4: When implementing the New Life Training in middle schools, the whole school students shall be divided into several teams (each team has 60 to 90 people) according to the establishment of scouts or military training. Each team shall have a mentor, who shall be appointed by the principal as a full-time teacher. However, the director of teaching or the director of moral education must also serve as a mentor for one team. Article 5: Under the mentor, each middle school shall divide students into several groups (each group has six to nine students). Each group shall have a group leader, who shall be appointed by the principal as a student with excellent learning and conduct. Under the guidance of the mentor, they shall be responsible for managing the students in the group. Article 6 When implementing the New Life Training in middle schools, the tasks of the principal are as follows: 1. Lead all training personnel in the school, lead by example, share weal and woe with students, and vigorously carry out personality influence; 2. Assess the work of all training personnel in the school; 3. Convene students to hold group lectures once a week, explaining the significance of the New Life and matters that should be noted and corrected; 4. Hold individual talks at any time to effectively guide students' lives; 5. Inspect students' classrooms, self-study rooms and work; 6. Supervise military training or scout training, as well as morning exercises or recess exercises; 7. Guide students' extracurricular activities and student autonomy; 8. Guide students' extracurricular reading and thinking; 9. Supervise students to tidy up and clean classrooms, self-study rooms and dormitories; 10. Handle student disputes; 11. Assess students' training results; 12. Implement student discipline; 13. Supervise the cleanliness of the whole school; 14. Contact student families and implement training; 15. Comprehensively manage other matters related to training students. Article 7: When implementing the New Life Training in middle schools, the director of teaching or the director of moral education shall assist the principal and bear the following tasks: 1. Practice the New Life, lead by example, share weal and woe with students, and vigorously carry out personality influence; 2. Convene students to hold group lectures once a week, explaining the significance of the New Life and matters that should be noted; 3. Hold individual talks at any time to effectively guide students' lives; 4. Inspect students' classrooms, self-study rooms and work; 5. Supervise military training or scout training, as well as morning exercises or recess exercises; 6. Guide students' extracurricular activities and student autonomy; 7. Guide students' extracurricular reading and thinking; 8. Supervise students to tidy up and clean classrooms, self-study rooms and dormitories; 9. Manage students' food and accommodation; 10. Handle student disputes; 11. Assess students' training results; 12. Examine students' cleanliness, hygiene, service discipline, courtesy, etc.; 13. Implement student rewards and punishments; 14. Contact student families and implement training; 15. Handle other matters related to training students. Article 8: The tasks of the mentors of each team in middle schools are as follows: 1. Practice the New Life, lead by example, share weal and woe with the students of this team, and vigorously carry out personality influence; 2. Assess the cleanliness, hygiene, service discipline, and courtesy of the students in this team; 3. Review the diaries of the students in this team; 4. Convene the students of this team to hold group lectures once a week, reporting the results of the assessment of the week and the matters that should be noted in the next week; 5. Hold individual talks at any time to effectively guide the lives of the students in this team; 6. Guide the extracurricular reading and thinking of the students in this team; 7. Supervise the self-study and extracurricular activities of the students in this team; 8. Supervise the military training or scout training and the morning exercises or recess exercises of the students in this team; 9. Supervise the students of this team to tidy up and clean the dormitories, self-study rooms and classrooms; 10. Manage the food and accommodation of the students of this team; 11. Handle disputes among the students of this team; 12. Examine the training results of the students of this team and report them to the principal on a monthly basis; 13. Implement student rewards and punishments; 14. Handle other matters related to training the students of this team. Article 9: The tasks of the group leaders of each group in middle schools are as follows: 1. Practice the New Life, lead by example, and be a model for the students of this group; 2. Examine the cleanliness, hygiene, service discipline, and courtesy of the students of this group on a daily basis, and report them to the mentor once a week; 3. Lead the students of this team to take turns tidying up and cleaning the dormitories, self-study rooms and classrooms; 4. Handle matters assigned by the principal, the director of teaching, the director of moral education, and the mentor.

3. Methods for Examining New Life Training Results

Article 10: Each middle school examines the new life training results of students. The group leaders of each group examine the lives of the students in their group on a daily basis according to the detailed items specified in Article 2, and report them to the mentor of their team on a weekly basis. Article 11: The mentors of each middle school assess the new life training results of each student on a monthly basis according to the results of the daily life examination of the students in their team, referring to the reports of the group leaders, and report them to the principal. The average of the monthly results is the training result of each student in the semester. Article 12: During the period of implementation of the New Life Training in each school, this result shall be used as the conduct result of each student.

4. Student Reward and Punishment Measures

Article 13: Students in middle schools who have excellent conduct results may adopt the following reward methods separately as rewards: 1. Public praise; 2. Merit; 3. Exemption from tuition fees; 4. Awarding books or other prizes; 5. Awarding medals. Article 14: Students in middle schools whose conduct results at the end of the month are above 80 points, or who have outstanding performance in the eight goals listed in Article 2, and are sufficient to be a model for all students in the school, should be publicly praised. Article 15: Students in middle schools who meet one of the following regulations should be given one merit: 1. Semester conduct result is above 80 points; 2. Diligent, frugal, clean, and strictly abide by the rules, and have never changed; 3. Academic subjects and conduct results are excellent, and the exams are always at the top; 4. Have not been absent from any subject in one semester, and can concentrate on learning; 5. Serve as a group leader, and their academic performance and conduct can be a model for all students in the school, and can be competent and responsible. Article 16: Students in middle schools who have been given two or more merits within one year may be exempted from tuition fees or given prizes and medals by the school to encourage them. Article 17: Students in middle schools who have low academic and conduct results may adopt the following punishment methods separately as warnings: 1. Verbal warning; 2. Written warning; 3. Demerit; 4. Retention; 5. Expulsion. Article 18: Students in middle schools who have one of the following facts should be given a verbal warning or a written warning as appropriate: 1. Conduct result at the end of the month is failing; 2. Have bad habits and do not change after persuasion; 3. Do not obey the guidance of the training personnel. Article 19: Students in middle schools who have one of the following facts should be given one demerit: 1. Semester conduct result is failing; 2. Lazy, unclean, and do not abide by school rules and do not change after three warnings; 3. Academic subjects and conduct results are low, and it is considered that there is no hope of progress; 4. Absent from academic subjects for more than one-third in one semester, or absent without reason for more than five times; 5. Holding the position of group leader, but not doing their job well and not accepting the guidance of the training personnel. Students who receive a demerit will have their position as group leader revoked at the same time. Article 20: Students in middle schools who have been given two or more demerits within one year will be given a retention or expulsion punishment by the school according to the severity of their laziness.

5. Methods for Contacting Student Families

Article 21: When implementing the New Life Training in middle schools, the school should print and send out the New Life Guidelines to urge each student's family to implement the New Life. Article 22: At the end of the semester, the middle school should list the conduct results, advantages and disadvantages of each student, and the matters that parents should pay attention to, and send them to each student's parents through the mentor. When rewarding or punishing students, the parents should also be notified at the same time. Article 23: The middle school should contact the families of the students with the best and worst academic performance at any time to provide various effective guidance. Article 24: The middle school should hold parent meetings or open house meetings regularly to report the guidance methods to the parents of the students, and to give lectures on the matters that parents should pay attention to.

6. Methods for Evaluating Training Personnel

Article 25: Principals of middle schools who have worked hard in supervising students' New Life Training and have achieved remarkable results will be given one merit after investigation by the Department of Education. Those who have been given two or more merits within one year will be given a certificate by the Department. Article 26: Principals of middle schools who have not worked hard in supervising students' New Life Training and have achieved poor results will be given one demerit after investigation by the Department of Education. Those who have been given two or more demerits within one year will be given a punishment by the Department as appropriate. Article 27: Directors of teaching or moral education and mentors of middle schools who have worked hard in students' New Life Training and have achieved remarkable results will be given one merit after investigation by the Department of Education. Those who have been given two or more merits within two years will be given a promotion or salary increase as appropriate. Article 28: Directors of teaching or moral education and mentors of middle schools who have not worked hard in students' New Life Training and have achieved poor results will be given one demerit after investigation by the Department of Education.

Those who have been given two or more demerits within one year will be given a salary reduction or dismissal as appropriate.

7. Supplementary Provisions

Article 29: This outline shall be promulgated and implemented by the Anhui Provincial Department of Education.

This Port

Total Report on the Number of Visitors to the Municipal Zoo: More Than 600,000 People Since It Opened 246

From August 1 to December 31 last year, the Shanghai Municipal Zoo was

open for a total of 131 days, except for exceptions.

The total number of visitors to the park was 640,749, with an average of 4,890 people per day. The day with the most visitors was National Ai Day, with a total of 13,730 people, with an average of 33 tickets sold per minute. The day with the fewest visitors was December

7, with a total of 594 people. This was due to the cold and heavy rain on that day.

The number of visitors in January this year was 60,617, and the number of visitors in February

was 104,110, and the number of visitors in March was 96,736.

Free Talk

Fiction and Essays 248

— Xu Maoyong

Fundamentally, perhaps also due to the emptiness of life, the novelists in China today generally strive for novelty and surprise in their work, whether in the subject matter, structure, sentence construction, or word choice. In my view, this is largely due to the influence of Japanese literature. Japan does not have great literature either, and this is also because its people do not have fulfilling lives. However, they are exceptionally clever, so they are flaunting their petty cleverness everywhere. The characteristics revealed in their literature are also novelty and surprise. One only needs to look at Mr. Zhou Zuoren's translation of "A Collection of Modern Japanese Short Stories" to understand this. In China, not only is literature deeply influenced by Japanese literature, but even ordinary writing has many Japanese-style elements. Originally empty content, coupled with a bit of novelty and surprise, becomes stimulating, satisfying the curiosity of those who are curious. This is like a woman whose spirit and body are completely depraved putting on a set of modern clothes.

The distinction between novels and essays also exists here. A novelist's observation of life is not enough to simply observe a certain special form; his eyes should see the more complete, more fundamental, and more universal aspects. Correspondingly, its expression should also be like this. An essayist is different. He often only sees an extremely small point on a whim, and then writes it out in epigrams. However, when writing, the essayist is clearly aware of his own emptiness, and also clearly confesses this to the reader. Otherwise, he would be writing a novel without measuring his own abilities. Therefore, for writers who cannot write novels but only write essays, critics, while mocking their emptiness and superficiality, should also forgive their honesty.

Unfortunately, our novelists also suffer from the emptiness of life, but what is even more painful is that they still have to write novels despite the emptiness of life. What can be done if there are no more complete, more fundamental, and more universal themes of life to write about in novels? They have to make people want to read them, so they have no choice but to make them essay-like: striving for novelty and surprise. Therefore, even if it is a very ordinary story narrated in the first person, as long as there are one or two epigrams in the middle, it becomes a novel.

The problem of "essayization of novels" pointed out by Mr. Mu Mutian is indeed very significant. But there is no way for "us" to "defend" against this trend. Because this is fundamentally due to the "emptiness of the writer's life," then what can "we" do except to say that the writers themselves should try their best to enrich their lives?

At the same time, I also hope that "essays" will not all be "easy literature." Writers with fulfilling lives can certainly write essays with the strength of a lion. To say that "prose essays" are definitely "products of the aristocratic or scholar-official class" is also a bit excessive. If the value of reportage literature is not erased by our critics, then its nature is actually very close to essays, feuilletons, and the like.

As for the question of a certain magazine editor mentioned by Mr. Mutian: "Recently, some things are simply indistinguishable as to whether they are novels or essays." then it is easy to solve. Those things are nothing more than two categories: one is definitely essays, and the other is neither novels nor essays.

Westward Journey Diary (10) 249

— Yu Dafu

After lunch, accompanied by the abbot, we all went up to the Sutra Dividing Platform on the high ground to the west. The platform is deserted and the temple is dilapidated, and it has now become a small thatched shed. Fifty steps west of the Sutra Dividing Platform, there is also a pool where Ge Hong refined elixirs, with a thatched shed on the pool and a monk practicing Taoism. When we arrived at the Sutra Dividing Platform, everyone's interest in sightseeing seemed to have been exhausted, but I, Jin Qianfu, Wu Shiji, and Xu Chengzhang became even more obsessed and determined to get to the bottom of things and climb to the very top of the Eastern Tianmu Mountain. Because the local chronicles say that the Western Tianmu Mountain is 3,500 zhang high, and the Eastern Tianmu Mountain is 3,900 zhang high. Once you are on the top of the Eastern Tianmu Mountain, you can see the shape of the mountains and rivers in half of Zhejiang Province clearly. Now that we have reached the Sutra Dividing Platform, which is eight-tenths of the way, who would be willing to give up the last bit of effort! After saying goodbye to the abbot and the other gentlemen who came with us, we only took a worker from the temple as a guide, cutting through thorns and brambles, crossing stone cliffs, and walking for two hours in the desolate grass and trees and on the muddy road before we reached the Great Immortal Peak, the summit of the Eastern Tianmu Mountain. According to the worker who accompanied us, the summit of the Immortal Peak is often covered by clouds and fog, and there are not many clear days in a year. Several years ago, the trees in the mountains were as thick as several arm spans and extended directly to the top of the mountain, so tigers, leopards, monkeys, and the like all lived there. Later, it was burned by a wildfire, and the entire mountain became scorched earth. After that, tigers and leopards disappeared, and the trees also disappeared. After hearing his words, we felt a little scared. Because after the fire, although only many withered trunks of large trees were left standing on the top of the mountain, the unburned thatch, wild bamboo, and the like had grown to a height of one person, and tigers, leopards, and the like could still hide there. After climbing over the Second Immortal Peak, the ground was full of dark water, and the grass was as wet as being by a stream. The worker said that this was the water flowing out of the Dragon Pool above, which would not dry up even in a severe drought. The higher we climbed, the thinner the air became, so everyone was panting heavily. When we arrived at the Immortal Affinity Stone, the scenery on all sides changed, and the enthusiasm of the four of us was even more exuberant.

This Immortal Affinity Stone is a large stone hundreds of zhang wide under the Dragon Pool on the Great Immortal Peak. There are countless strangely shaped rock walls and caves. The top of the Immortal Affinity Stone is directly under that steep cliff, which is the Dragon Pool. Although it is a small pool of clear water in the stone wall, the overflow can help form the flying foam and silver waves of the east and west waterfalls. It is not surprising that the villagers regard this as a god. Moreover, the Eastern Mountain Chronicle also records the story of people in the past encountering immortals on this stone, so later generations wrote poems comparing this stone to Liu and Ruan's Tiantai Mountain. But we neither saw dragons nor encountered immortals, only sat for a long time under an old pine tree on a rock resembling a lion on the east side of the Immortal Affinity Stone—this pine tree was really strange, it was not burned in the fire——sitting and resting under this solitary pine tree, looking up at the azure sky and the setting sun, and the surrounding valleys and cliffs, although we could not become immortals, each of our stomachs was full of feelings, a bit floaty as if we were drunk.

Mr. Zhou Zuoren's Self-Congratulatory Poem 250

— Cao Juren

- The Road from Kong Rong to Tao Yuanming

The publication of Mr. Zhou Zuoren's fiftieth birthday poem in the "Human World" magazine has aroused much criticism; the poem is good, and the criticism is also correct.

The Zhou family legend says that Mr. Zhou's previous life was an old monk: Mr. Zhou also claimed to have obtained a poem in a dream: "Resting in the meditation hall, bathing outside the meditation hall, although there are differences in movement and stillness, the mind is idle and there is no obstacle." Reincarnation as a monk, "there is definite evidence." Mr. Zhou's recent tranquil life, separated from monks by a leisure time, and compared with the ancients, is closest in state of mind to Tao Yuanming. Zhu Xi said, "Hermits are mostly people with a strong temperament and resentment," Tao Yuanming was indifferent to the outside world, but what he yearned for were figures like Tian Zita and Jing Ke. The fire in his heart, although under the cold ashes, was still burning fiercely. Mr. Zhou retreated from the front line of the New Literature Movement to talk about foxes and ghosts in the Bitter Rain Studio. Did he really become tired of the world and coldly watch? Presumably, the fierce fire is still burning under the cold ashes. Some time ago, Mr. Zhou wrote to Mr. Yu Pingbo, saying: "I also saw middle school students gave a lecture with Yu Tong, considering me as a school in literature, I disagree with this humble opinion, but this can still be said to be a matter of seeing benevolence and wisdom; only to say that I still maintain the demeanor of the May Fourth era is a big mistake. A person's attitude towards life changes all the time, how can it be maintained for thirteen or fourteen years? I examine myself and find that my thinking has become more and more decadent recently, how can I still have the impetuous and fierce energy of the May Fourth era?" From "impetuous and fierce" to "decadent thinking," in the eyes of others, it is of course like another world.

This path of ideological change can be called "the road from Kong Rong to Tao Yuanming."

Among the Jian'an literati, Kong Rong was indignant and out of step with the world. He couldn't stand what he saw, and he always loved to say it. He loved to contradict Cao Cao and scratch Cao Cao's itch, and was finally killed by Cao Cao. Those of the same generation as Kong Rong, such as Mi Heng and Yang Xiu, fell into the same fate. A little later, the Sima family came to power, and it was especially difficult to be a person: The Biography of Ruan Ji says, "During the transition between the Wei and Jin dynasties, the world was in turmoil, and few scholars were able to survive." Therefore, ordinary intellectuals had to anesthetize their souls, drink wine and take medicine to preserve their lives. Like Ruan Ji, "he did not engage in worldly affairs, and being drunk was the norm. Zhong Hui asked him about current affairs several times, wanting to convict him based on his approval or disapproval, but he always got away with it because he was drunk." However, He Yan and Ji Kang still could not escape, and even anesthetizing themselves was not allowed. Some time later, Buddhist thought became popular, and all anger was extinguished; the world-renouncing view replaced the world-affirming view, and intellectuals all became figures like Tao Yuanming. Mr. Zhou's thoughts in the May Fourth era need no further explanation. In 1926, Mr. Zhou saw the news that Sun Chuanfang had beheaded fifty students in Jiujiang, and wrote a letter to Mr. Chi Guang, saying; "Brother Chi Guang, today I saw in the English newspaper in the Yanjing University Library that Sun Chuanfang had beheaded fifty students in Jiujiang, and that ten students were sentenced to death in a certain place. I couldn't help but think of a short poem by the Greek pessimistic poet Baladas. (Original poem omitted) The poem roughly means that we are all watched and fed, like a group of pigs, to be slaughtered at will by the god of death. --However, the god of death is an alien, and people cannot do anything to him. People treating people as pigs is shocking, although there was the allusion of human swine in ancient times."

His anger is evident in his words. But since that time, he closed his doors to read books, and Dumb's Praise came out. Except for the Prisoner's Record in the Women's College, we no longer saw words with impetuous and fierce energy. Mr. Zhou has experienced world changes and is willing to hide his talent and preserve himself by living as a hermit. This is probably inevitable. Mr. Zhou's ideological changes in the past ten years are precisely a microcosm of the ideological changes between Kong Rong and Tao Yuanming in the two hundred years; after reading the self-congratulatory poem, we can understand it even more clearly!

"Postscript"

Mr. Yutang,

Mr. Zhou's self-congratulatory poem is respectfully written on Jiliu Xuan paper,

It is exquisitely mounted by a Suzhou mounter and hung in the Lin family's study, where we can appreciate it together. This method is the most appropriate and saves a lot of trouble. What do you think?

A Tentative Translation of the Book of Songs 251

— Yu Shixia

The Mountain Has a Pivot (1)

There is a tree on the mountain called the pivot,

There is a tree at the foot of the mountain called the elm.

You have clothes,

Not trailing, not embracing.

You have carriages and horses,

Not galloping, not driving.

The day you die,

Others will be very happy!

(2)

There is a tree on the mountain called the kao,

There is a tree at the foot of the mountain called the niu.

You have halls,

You display bells and drums,

Not striking, not knocking.

The day you die,

Others will be very rich!

(3)

There is a tree on the mountain called lacquer,

There is a tree at the foot of the mountain called chestnut.

You have wine and food,

Why not play the zither every day?

Let's be happy and joyful for now,

Let's spend the long days like this for now.

The day you die,

Others will openly enter your house!

Yunnan Folk Songs 252

— Su Jimin

(1) Getting up early to walk to my sister's house,

My sister's house has thin rice cooked with pumpkin;

Thinking of asking my brother to stay for a meal,

There are still my two parents in front of the hall.

(2)

The lover wants to go, and the sister wants to stay,

Bitter buckwheat cakes wrapped in lard,

Opening it halfway,

My sister's heart is inside.

New York Correspondence (4) 253

— Luo Chifeng

(2) Sing a Low Down Tune (Sing a Low Down Tune)

Little New Asia Lee, sing a low down tune,

Beside the cherry tree, under the faint moon, the little Chinese child is coming, sing a low down tune.

········

Little New Asia Lee, learns the ah tune, like an American, can dance the same way. It's not difficult to get the lover's heart, the lover will say:

Sing a low down tune.

········

Little Chinese child is coming soon, when you hug him tightly, under the moon, sing a low down tune.

········

(3) Who's Gonna Wash Your Clothes (Who's Gonna Laundry) This song was popular in Shanghai during the Sino-Japanese War. It was a speculative work. After the Sino-Japanese War, no one sang it anymore.

Everyone is worried,

Spending time in worry, those who are worried,

They haven't even heard of anything. We should really be glad,

That terrible thing has not yet come.········

Who's gonna wash your clothes,

When your Chinaman goes to the front to fight?

When he's fighting the Japanese in a bloody battle, who's gonna launder your underwear?

·······

I know who will shine your shoes, that's the shoe shiner's job. But who's gonna wash your clothes, when your Chinaman is fighting on the front?

·····

(4) Not for All the Rice in China (Not for all the rice in China)

·······

Not for all the rice in China,

Not for all the grapes in France, I would lightly give up the joy of dancing with you.

·······

Not for all the kilts in Scotland, not for all the bulls in Spain, (although you're driving me crazy,) I would give up the chance to meet you.

·······

Not for all the leeks in the Pemi Valley, not for all the cheese in Switzerland, I would exchange your sweet kisses with others.

·······

Not for all the beans in Boston, not for all the meat slices in Montreal, I would lightly give up the happiness of our union.

Mother (5) 254

— Luo Hong

The beautiful image of his deceased wife was clearly reflected in his mind again. He explained to himself that this remarriage could not be regarded as forgetting her. If she could understand his difficulties, she would not be harsh on him!

From that day on, in the children's hearts, they often thought of that new mother. The older child had heard that her cousin's stepmother treated her very cruelly, and her cousin often shed tears in secret. Several of her classmates also had stepmothers, and they all said that their stepmothers did not treat them well, so she was very doubtful in her heart. She wondered, would Ligu treat them badly? Would Ligu be like other people's stepmothers, often scolding them, not allowing them to eat good things, and not allowing them to be happy? But Dad said that Ligu must love them very much. Then would Ligu be like her own mother, holding her sister, caressing herself, and singing soft lullabies? Sometimes her mother made very good snacks and shared them with them. Even when her mother was very angry, she never scolded or beat her. After her mother died, the child slowly forgot about her. Now Dad said that they would have a new mother, so her memory of her mother became deeper than when she had just died, and it was also the first time she felt the pain of not having a mother!

"Brother, when will Ligu come to be our mother!" her sister asked him once.

"I don't know!"

"Is she the same as our mother?"

"I don't know either!"

The sister glanced at her brother and ran away angrily.

He really wanted to ask his father when Ligu would come to be their mother; but he wanted to ask several times, but he never did, because he felt that his father was not the same father as before. His father no longer talked to him about this and that with the same childish excitement. When he was studying, his father no longer often looked at him and asked him many questions. Although his father was still so kind and happy, he did not talk as much as before, and often stared at him blankly for a while. He did not understand why his father had become like this.

Originally, the father had to change a bouquet of fresh flowers in front of the mother's portrait every day. The father would never let the maid do this. The father personally inserted a bouquet of fresh flowers in the vase every day, and was satisfied only when the bouquet of flowers looked good to the father. And he had also seen the father change the vase three times. The father had told him that when the mother was alive, she liked to arrange all the furniture beautifully, and often liked to change the style of the house, so the father would change it for the mother when he had a better-looking vase. But these past few days, the father no longer changed fresh flowers for the mother every day. After the first bouquet of fresh flowers withered, Aunt Lu told the father to throw them away, so he threw them away, and he never inserted them again. The father had repeatedly told them: "No matter what, you must never forget your mother!" But, hasn't Dad forgotten first? he thought. Originally, every three weeks, the father always took them to the cemetery to see the day when the mother was buried. The cemetery was not very far from home, so they went to see their mother on the one hand, and took the opportunity to take a walk on the other. Yesterday was also the day to go, but the father said that he had urgent matters and changed it to next week! This matter made the sister the most angry. She had been looking forward to this walk for a long time, but it was stopped by her father.

Grain: Futures Flour Short Sellers Profit and Cover 266

Yesterday, after the flour market opened in the morning, the market for each month turned up and stabilized. Since foreign wheat quotations, Chicago rose by about three, four, and six tenths of a corner, and Ella rose by three corners and three tenths on the right, after the opening, the sentiment for near and far months seemed to turn favorable. Furthermore, because after the gradual plunge last week, the difference in the market has reached six, seven, and eight points, profit-taking accounts are thinking of covering their positions. Therefore, the buying sentiment was very strong for a while, and the price also rose step by step. Until the afternoon opening, it was initially seen as stable, but then, because customers from various gangs were quite absorbing May contracts, and short covering was still in progress, the market turned up again. However, small factories had gradually released their inventories, so the ending trend showed a slack again. As a result, this month was better by one point compared to last week, May to August was better by one point and seven tenths of a cent, and September was better by one point.

Futures Wheat Initially Up, Then Tired 267

Yesterday, after the opening of the futures wheat market in the morning, the market for each month showed an initial uptrend followed by stability. Since foreign wheat quotations, both places are estimated to have recovered by three, four, and six tenths of a corner, the sentiment after the opening was expensive, and the asking price for each month was better by about two, three, and four points compared to the previous week. After entering, because buyers were not abundant, it turned to a tired trend again. Until the afternoon opening, because the selling sentiment recovered and mainland gangs slightly released their inventories, each month showed a falling image. This month, due to delivery being near, the current inventory is still flat, and the price is gradually falling and not stopping. As a result, this month fell by four points, June was unchanged, and July and August were both down by one point. It is said that the current wheat has not yet been opened because the factory appetite has not opened.

Silk and Tea 270

Rainy Weather Does Not Hinder Young Silkworms

"Chang'an" This year's farmers' hatching and breeding is not weak, but the collection of ants is insufficient. After opening and discarding, the weather is too cold, and the development is stagnant. Instructors are running around to care for them, and there is no damage. The early gangs have already started the third sleep, while the late gangs have only been open and discarded for four or five mornings. It rained the night before last, but fortunately, the young have little impact. "Farmers in the four townships of Fuyang, due to unfavorable breeding in recent years, the number of this year's silkworm ants is not smooth, only two-thirds of last year. After opening and discarding, the silkworm ants eat and discard slowly due to the cold weather, and the development is not good. The weather has been sunny and warm in recent days, and the current condition of silkworm ants is excellent. The heavy rain the day before yesterday finally stopped, and households all dried the rain-soaked silkworms, and there was no change. The early gangs have already had enough sleep for two, and the late gangs are also open and discarded for two." "Pinghu" silkworm affairs are about ten days later than Hangzhou. Farmers are now preparing for hatching and breeding. The early ones have already reached the stage of urging green and discarding, and the late gangs can also produce ants within days. The instructors are now disinfecting the silkworm houses for the farmers. "Wuxi" Instructors in the four townships of Wuxi are promoting silkworm affairs and distributing improved seeds to farmers, advising them to hatch and breed, and disinfecting the silkworm houses on behalf of them. In a few days, they can collect ants. This year's silkworm affairs in Xiyi, due to the farmers' intentions and the amount of restrictive regulations, have been reduced, and the future is difficult to be optimistic.

Wenzhou Black Tea Has Opened the Scale 271

Wenzhou black tea has already started picking in recent days. The quality of this new head tea is still not bad. The opening price of rough tea is 45 yuan per dan. It seems that the cost of manufacturing and transporting it to Shanghai in the future will be heavier than in previous years.

Local Tea Factories are Launching Weighing Operations One After Another 272

Local tea factories in this port, in view of the fact that new teas from the mainland are about to be harvested, and in order to seek quick business operations, are sparing no effort in the purchase of goods. Yesterday, it was heard that tea houses such as Changji Gongsheng have all sent personnel to Sui'an, Shaoxing and other places, and the situation is quite enthusiastic.

Hangzhou Tea Market is Booming 273

Hangzhou is the concentration of shop and tea businesses. In recent days, various green teas from Zhejiang, such as Longjing, Shifeng, Maofeng, and Yuqian, have been listed sporadically. Among them, Longjing and Maofeng are in great demand due to the large appetite of Shanghai gangs, and the daily shipments are in short supply. Transactions of other various new teas are also not lonely. As for the selling prices of each tea, Longjing has opened up to 660 yuan, Maoyufeng Qian has opened a new price of 280 yuan, and Shilefeng's selling price is 320 yuan. The market is quite booming.

New Voice of She-Tun Tea Market 274

She County: Green tea from She County has always been divided into foreign firm "Rain" grade and domestic shop "Zhuang" grade. The total amount of production and sales is roughly equal. Historically, the domestic shops "Zhuang" started earlier than the foreign firms, so the tea shops opened in various ports within the country were all managed by She County people. Before the fall of the Northeastern provinces, the jasmine-scented green tea and tea dust produced in She County sold very well and business was good. Although the Northeastern provinces have been cut off in recent years, the sales markets in North China, Shandong, and Hebei have not declined significantly and can still maintain their former status. This year's new tea is about to arrive as the Grain Rain solar term approaches, and Huangshan Maofeng tea will soon be harvested. Recently, Tianjin tea firms such as Zheng Xingde and Zheng Ji have sent personnel with funds to She County to purchase tea. Shandong tea merchants have also increased compared to previous years. However, since the beginning of spring, the weather has been cold and rainy, and the tea buds have been frozen by the cold air, resulting in slow growth. The date of new tea hitting the market will be later than in previous years. As for the foreign tea firms, there has been no increase or decrease in number this year. Currently, all the firms prioritize medium- and low-grade tea leaves for export, taking a proactive approach to tea business, and the market seems to be quite lively.

Tunxi: As the center of the Anhui tea market, tea shops line up in one corner. In the most prosperous years, there were about eighty or ninety shops, and in the quiet years, there were still fifty or more. The rise and fall of the tea market in the producing area depends on the increase or decrease of tea shops and the expansion or contraction of purchases. Last year, due to losses from the previous two shipments, there were only about fifty tea shops in the Tunxi market. Fortunately, the cost was slightly lower, the management was cautious, and the business performance was better than in previous years. Although the profits were not abundant, few suffered losses. This year, all the original tea shops continue to open, and the number of newly organized shops has increased by more than ten. In total, there are about seventy old and new tea shops preparing to enter the market. All the tea factories in the nearby areas have been rented out. According to people in the industry, the boxed tea made in Tunxi last year has already been sold out. This year, with the convenience of transportation on the Hangzhou-Anhui Railway, they can gain an advantage in business. Even if the market changes in the future, they can adjust their sails according to the wind and avoid the danger of running aground. Therefore, the booming of Tunxi tea shops this year is based on a pre-determined plan for advance and retreat.

Tremendous Drop of Over Ten Yuan in North-South Goods and Orchid Bamboo Branches 275

Since the beginning of spring, the sales of orchid bamboo branches have been sluggish, and the market has been depressed for a long time. The shops, seeing no hope for a turnaround in the future, have found it useless to hold on. Therefore, they have recently been selling off their stocks, with prices dropping from twenty-six or twenty-seven yuan to twenty-two or twenty-three yuan, and then to seventeen or eighteen yuan. A total of over two hundred boxes have been sold, and the price has plummeted by more than ten yuan compared to the prices earlier in the year. It is rumored that this shipment was purchased by merchants from Hangzhou.

Extra Edition of Shen Bao in this City

Discussion

The Dead End of Disarmament 276

— Bin Fu

Who says only Chinese people are forgetful? Aren't all people in the world forgetful? The cruel lessons of the Great War, barely twenty years ago, have already been completely forgotten by people. Isn't it so? The imperialist powers are once again frantically expanding their weapons of war, preparing for a second great massacre. In the Far East, in Central Europe, isn't every place filled with ominous clouds of war?

However, while they are so enthusiastically expanding their armaments, they are also sending many "gentlemen" wearing top hats and white gloves to Geneva to discuss disarmament. This is truly a remarkable feat of forgetfulness!

The so-called disarmament conference has been going on for more than two years, from February 1932 to the present. What has it actually accomplished? No one can answer this question. We only know that this conference spent 350 million gold pounds last year alone, which is an astonishing waste! In addition, some "memoranda" and "notes" could probably be piled up into a mountain.

This is not an exaggeration. Just looking at the documents exchanged by European countries regarding disarmament in March, according to Mr. Henderson, who holds the "fattest job in the world" (isn't the chairman of the disarmament conference the fattest job in the world? His salary is provided by all the countries of the world, yet he can do nothing), the gentleman who recently convened a main committee meeting in Geneva took the following from his briefcase:

(1) Memorandum from France to Germany on February 14

(2) Eden's conversations with Italy

(3) Memorandum from Germany to France on March 13

(4) Memorandum from France to England on March 19

(5) Memorandum from England to France on April 10

(6) Memorandum on disarmament from small countries on April 14

(7) Memorandum from Germany to England on April 16

However, even though the "memoranda" are as numerous as snowflakes, the imperialist powers have not improved their memory in the slightest. They are only planning how to increase the strength of their own armies. Their so-called disarmament is just a hope to disarm other countries' armies, while their own country's army should remain intact. As Berne said: "They don't even pretend to disarm, they just hope to come up with cheaper methods. In Geneva, they are just discussing with each other: 'Well, a sixteen-inch shell is much more expensive than a ten-inch shell. I'm thinking of replacing the sixteen-inch shell with a ten-inch shell to hit you, what do you think?' The success of the disarmament conference is entirely built on this kind of meaning."

In this way, hoping for the success of the disarmament conference is simply a pipe dream.

To implement disarmament, it is clear that conferences cannot succeed, nor can any "memoranda" or "notes" be effective. As Radek said well:

"Now there is only one kind of treaty that can still be concluded, that is, a treaty for the great powers to use to replace the League of Nations to discuss burying the disarmament conference and eliminating the difficulties for new armaments."

On May 30, the General Commission on Disarmament will meet again. We will hear the final death knell of disarmament at that time. ·22·

The Harm of "Obsession" 277

— Bo Er

Some people say: Life in this world is just an obsession. True, precisely because it is an obsession, we need to uncover this obsession, because obsession is the greatest harm. Here, we can cite various obsessions in society as examples to first understand the harm of obsession, and then understand the necessity of a life dedicated to uncovering this obsession.

Obsession with Gods—Religion: I say it is a tool for inner cultivation. Jesus said: Repent and you will be saved. Buddha also has this kind of teaching: Good people are rewarded, and bad people are punished. The meaning of both Buddha and Jesus is to hope that people in the world will not commit crimes or do bad things. However, after years and months of storytelling, people regard Buddha and Jesus as living gods who can cure all diseases. Even religions that claim to be civilized and more advanced, such as Christianity, still have this kind of superstition. Look, when their son is seriously ill, they don't call a doctor, but kneel in front of the child's bed to pray, believing that Jesus will save their innocent child. When the son cannot live and dies, they say that it is Jesus's intention to let their son go to heaven to enjoy happiness. This clearly shows the harm of obsession. If they didn't blindly believe that Jesus could save the child's life, wouldn't it be possible for the doctor to use medicine to cure him? Therefore, if Christianity desperately spreads to uneducated people in the countryside, making them blindly believe without reason, I believe the world's population increase and decrease problem will be affected.

Obsession with Women—We cannot but admit that there is a group of women-obsessed people in society. They have wives—not enough, they also have concubines, starting from number zero to number eighty-six—not enough, they also have mistresses, prostitutes, and dance partners, all of whom they have to meet secretly every day; as a result, with their limited energy, they are obsessed with the realm of women. Therefore, they have no pure love for their wives, no sense of responsibility for teaching and raising children, and at the same time, their money is completely wasted. This is the second practical evidence of the harm of obsession.

In addition, there are also sports obsessives, reading obsessives, opera obsessives, gambling obsessives, and drinking obsessives. Most sports obsessives are school students. They only know sports and don't know how to read. In the future, after graduating from school (those who are specially allowed to graduate due to outstanding sports performance), they want to find a career in society, but even writing love letters to their lovers requires begging friends to write for them. Naturally, it is not easy for them to find a suitable position in society. All they have is a bit of strength and two long, thick, red legs. Then go be a dock worker, but they are upright scholars, who would have thought that they would end up unable to write or fight! I dare to say here that they are no different from a yellow cow, obeying the farmer's command, and can run hundreds of meters in an empty field. Reading obsessives also have bad places. Originally, reading more books is the best, but once you are obsessed, it is harmful to your health. Opera obsessives, gambling obsessives, and drinking obsessives lose both money and spirit at the same time, which are also the faults of obsession.

After talking about so many obsessions above, I still feel that there is one obsession that cannot be ignored. What is this obsession? It is the most fashionable obsession. I say it is the obsession with being an official. The idea of becoming an official has unknowingly invaded the minds of every young person, especially when they reach university. They are not good at studying knowledge in school. What they think about day and night is how they can become officials after leaving school. Therefore, university has become a preparation period for becoming officials, wasting good youthful years. This is indeed an obsession with being an official! But, what is so good about being an official? Naturally, this is the model given to them by the officials of our country in the past. Officials have always been rich. Not only can they have money as they wish, but they can also exercise power as they wish. Therefore, isn't being an official a pleasant thing? Who wouldn't want to be powerful too?

The Problem of Prostitution Prohibition 278

— Ms. Jiong

We know that the existence of prostitutes in society is not accidental, but is bred by this deformed socio-economic organization. This is something that no one can deny. Although Morgan Lewis H. Morgan believed that "the institution of prostitution is the shadow cast by the past on present family life." Or say, "The institution of prostitution is probably a remnant of ancient cross-pollination, or a symbolic memory." As for the abolition of this institution of prostitution, it is considered an important topic in social problems. In the past, in cities all over the world, passive abolition or active prohibition has been proposed, but the result has been in vain! Because the problem of prohibiting prostitution cannot be completely resolved until the socio-economic organization has undergone new changes and been established! Unexpectedly, after being frustrated by the resolution of the Sino-Japanese issue, the League of Nations vaguely proposed - and even "decided" - on a motion to "prohibit prostitution worldwide."

Geneva, November 11, National Electric Report:

"The League of Nations decided to ban all brothels in the world. ... The report on which it is based details that there are official and private prostitutes in major cities around the world. It is not difficult to prohibit this kind of improper business as long as the authorities do not issue licenses. ... Some believe that after the prohibition of prostitution, if they change their faces, it will inevitably lead to no way to investigate. However, if they can be given proper occupations after the prohibition of prostitution, they will naturally be able to become good people."

This "official article" looks rigorous, strong, straightforward, and reasonable on the surface, but in reality, it is just a "meaningless document"! Because the core of the problem lies in whether the authorities of each country can "give them proper occupations" so that they can "become good people"!

Let's see... The hurricane of the current world economic panic is raging... The commercial depression, rural bankruptcy, and the sharp increase in the number of unemployed people are at the end of this century! The authorities of each country are trying to make up for the deficit in the east and west to maintain their economic foundation, and they have no time to deal with the millions of skilled unemployed workers suffering from hunger and cold, let alone these prostitutes?

However, we are even more impressed by the self-destruction of prostitution after the Soviet Union completed the five-year plan in four years in a new corner of the earth - the Soviet Union, which makes us feel that "it is not difficult to prohibit as long as the authorities do not issue licenses." The emptiness of this superficial theory! Because the problem of prohibiting prostitution, according to past experiences, cannot be solved by superficial treatment; but requires thinking from the root. That is to say... If you want to eliminate prostitutes in major cities around the world, you should first investigate the reasons for the formation of the institution of prostitution since ancient times, and the conditions for the existence of prostitution under the current social system, and then you can propose a plan to prohibit prostitution.

Here, we deeply feel that prostitution exists with social organization and economic system, which is called "coexistence and co-prosperity"! Therefore, if you want to prohibit prostitution all over the world, you have to abandon this old socio-economic organization and create a new one. It is definitely not something that the League of Nations can do with such a "meaningless document."

Seeking Spring 279

— Wen Hei

Spring has been in the world for a while, living in the alley of the city, not seeing red flowers and green grass, not hearing the singing of birds, after all, living here only has the feeling of hot and cold climate, and does not distinguish between spring and autumn. The pavilion room has no sun, and is isolated from nature! Although there are some landscape paintings hanging on the wall, and there is also a calligraphy scroll given to me by the painter, saying, "Vulgar guests do not come to the courtyard, the thatched door is set up but never closed; in the small window all day there is nothing to do, imitating Ni Zan and Huang Gongwang's mountains after the rain." However, only the mountain after the rain in the painting gives me a little feeling of spring. Recently, it happened to be a few days of drizzling spring rain, which was suffocating. Today, the sky is clear, so I really want to go to the countryside to see if spring has really come, so I went out after lunch. Longhua Temple's peach blossoms are originally a good way to seek spring, but when I think of the cars of famous ladies and gentlemen passing by you, even if you are unmoved and follow the etiquette, integrity, and shame of the New Life Movement, "do not look at what is impolite," you will still have a face full of dust and eat a nose full of ash on the side of the road. Therefore, I decided to go to the Jiangwan countryside to find a friend, and I shouldn't be unable to find spring in the vegetable garden and meadow there, right? I live in the south, so to get to the Jiangwan countryside, I must go north, so the road between the north and south ends is not too far. After changing trams several times, I finally arrived at the entrance of Jiangkou Park. Outside the gate, the trees by the fence were green, and the grass in the park was also green, but I didn't see a flower. I thought to myself: Spring has really come after all. But seeing a spring without flowers is enough to be melancholy! Just as I turned a corner and advanced towards Jiangwan, I saw several Japanese soldiers carrying rifles shouting and running fast, and subconsciously felt the arrival of disaster, and immediately stopped and dared not move forward. The Japanese soldiers rushed left and right, passing from the telephone pole on this side of the road to the telephone pole along the railway line, practicing street fighting. The interest in seeking spring was shattered by this scene of the tragic future drama reminiscent of the "January 28th" incident, and I had to return to the city melancholy and wandered in the tide of people and cars.

I have no spring in my heart, and I don't even have the fate to seek spring. I should be doing the buried work of earning a living in a cold and gloomy pavilion room. Alas.

Qing Qing 280

— Wang Wei

Today, I unintentionally received Qing Qing's letter, and I miss Qing Qing again; Qing Qing's letter is like this: Mr. Wang: How are you? Why did you have to go back in the middle of the night yesterday? After you left, who will play the harmonica for me when I perform the dance today? Mr. Wang, you look too much like my dead older brother. My older brother in the past also had a kind smile like yours; he also liked me like you; he could also play the harmonica very well. Mr. Wang, I want to call you older brother, can you promise me?

Older brother, I must come to the school you teach in the second half of the year to study. I really want to live with older brother often! I wish you

Happiness, Your newly acquainted little friend: Qing Qing

Qing Qing is like a flower in my consciousness; a white flower.

The day before yesterday, Qing Qing's school held a school celebration carnival; I met Qing Qing in the dressing room. As soon as I ran into the dressing room, Qing Qing jumped up from the sofa, wearing a fluttering dance suit; she embraced me, smiling so adorably, smiling. "Qing Qing, this is Mr. Wang, who I told you about!" Their principal introduced her like this. "Mr. Wang," Qing Qing called softly, leaning against me like a sheep: "Mr. Wang, you really look like my older brother."

"Then, you can call me older brother!" I smiled at her, stroking her soft hair. "Mr. Wang, how about playing a harmonica for me to listen to?" Her voice was soft. "Okay! I'll play while you dance?" She lowered her head and smiled, "Is "Swallows Flying Together" okay?" "Okay!"

So, I started playing the tune - she sang and danced... like a nightingale. At the end, she flew into my arms like a dance, and said shyly:

"Not dancing well! Not dancing well!"

I thought to myself, "Gentle little girl!" She told me many things about her school, and also told me about the program she performed today.

The stage opened - whenever she danced, I always played the music for her.

When the show ended, the night was already so deep; I wanted to go back, but Qing Qing dragged me, begging me. "Mr. Wang! Don't go back! Teach at our school!"

"Qing Qing, this is not possible; if you miss me, I will come to see you often in the future!" I held her hand.

She looked at my face disappointedly, as if she was about to cry.

I picked her up and whispered in her ear...

"Qing Qing, don't be sad, your older brother must go tonight." After I put Qing Qing down, I left hastily.

Today, I unintentionally received Qing Qing's letter, and I miss Qing Qing again.

Qing Qing is like a flower in my mind, a white flower.

Vanished Youth 281

— Mai Fu

One of the most embarrassing things on weekdays is when people ask about "age".

Although I have never lied, and there is no need to make my age younger, I always have to say one or two years older. However, the listeners never believe it. Judging from the questioning expression, they always think that my answer is incorrect. Sometimes people even praise me like this... "Such a young child!" This makes me feel unusually embarrassed, because I know that although I am young, my appearance is indeed a bit old. The wrinkles on my forehead and the paleness of my face have clearly marked my position in life. Those who praise me as a young child are undoubtedly mocking me.

To tell the truth, I am only twenty-three years old this year, but I look like a middle-aged man in his thirties. I don't care about this. It's okay to be old. Life always gets old. What does it matter! However, my age is indeed young, but I am so severely aging, which is still sad!

Why am I so old? I can only scold my environment. At sixteen, I was sick at home for the whole year, but it was not serious, because I was too old. Most families didn't even have food to eat, so my father was very neglectful of my illness. He hired a doctor to see me once or twice, but it didn't get better, so he stopped. This dragged on, so eating medicine was rarely effective. In the end, my mother specially ran around and raised a larger amount of medical expenses to take medicine non-stop to eliminate the illness. However, at this time, my body has suffered a great blow. I was only seventeen years old, but I looked like someone in their twenties. I vaguely remember that in the spring of 1927, a cousin got married, and I went to make trouble in the bridal chamber. Probably because I made too much trouble, the bride pleaded like this... "Please let this old man rest for a while!" This made me very angry. I was only seventeen years old, and she said I was an old man, so I made even more unruly trouble until she knelt down and worshipped. However, at that time, there was infinite sadness in my heart, because youth was indeed saying goodbye to me, although I had not really become an old man.

In the past few years, I have been living in Shanghai, and the life I have lived makes me dare not recall it. Sometimes I am full of poverty, and sometimes I have suffered enough insults from the dogs. The worst thing is that I worked as a slave under Mr. X for the whole year in 1920, and last year I didn't breathe air for the whole year. I have also suffered several mild or severe illnesses.

These are the roots of ruining my youth. Under this kind of torture, I had long planned that I didn't want my youth, and in fact it couldn't stay.

However, although the appearance is a bit old, the mood is fortunately still youthful. This, I can guarantee with confidence.

As long as my heart is indeed youthful, I also feel that I am still a salvageable person. Yes, the dangerous environment, the dangerous society, I must give it a worthy reward.

Random Thoughts 282

— Yi Ying

Quiet in the window, the sun is fading, the incense in the incense burner is gone, but the fire is still warm; leaning lazily on the embroidered bed, deeply closing the door, eyes blurry, half-open, half-dozing.

Tired of listening to the wild sparrows chirping on the carved eaves, afraid of seeing the willow catkins flutter on the embroidered curtains; picking up the embroidery needle and turning it upside down, the two tips pointing, half-relaxed, half-gathered. - Zha Deqing - Occasionally I flipped through a collection of Yuan Dynasty songs, and these two are my favorites and I can't bear to let go. I silently recited them several times, and a little spring heart couldn't help but feel a great surge. It's as if an ancient war is a desperate war for weak nations.

The Tramp Child - Produced by Chen Jingsheng 283

War is terrifying, but surrender is by no means a spring-dreaming beauty, emerging gracefully from the book, "Smiling, leaning on the jade youth, wanting to sleep," I immediately regard myself as the powdered youth.

Imagination cannot but allow me to trace back to centuries ago. The mystery of the relationship between men and women is truly thought-provoking. In the secluded boudoir, a maiden harboring spring desires is locked away, her heart full of spring feelings with nowhere to express them, and she has no choice but to entrust them to the surrounding scenery. The blooming and falling of flowers touch her heart with joy and sorrow; the waxing and waning of the moon evoke endless longing. Wisps of incense and the murmuring of swallows are enough to make her feel envy, jealousy, and resentment. At this time, everything feels unnatural... Sitting is not right, standing is not good, just soft and languid, an indescribable emotion that even the most skilled artist cannot capture even a fraction of. "Since the flowers

three four, rambling on, half true, half frivolous." A poem that truly captures this feeling.

Even if there is a matter of secret love, it is always done stealthily, the so-called "moon on the willow tip, a rendezvous after dusk" is enough to exquisitely portray the essence of a tryst. As for "Wearing spring clouds, loosening jade hairpins, eyebrows faint like autumn mountains in a mirror, is the crabapple in bloom? Is the powdered youth coming?" this poem can even make me think of a mysterious circle of a maiden in a deep boudoir longing for spring.

"A jade beauty leans lazily against the east wind in the spring slumber" is, after all, real, as for things like "The spring scenery cannot be contained in the garden, a branch of red apricot extends over the wall," how much of that can there really be? In this regard, I have always preferred mystery. If humanity reaches the point of unrestrained freedom like cats calling for spring, what meaning is there left? However, the giant wheel of the times eventually carries humanity down this path. Clothes can be discarded, and naked you face me, and I face you, calling it "returning to nature." I don't believe why no one advocates eating raw meat and drinking blood, wouldn't that be even closer to "nature"?

Things like this really frighten me. I remember once seeing these words in a tabloid: "If women don't wear pants, men will inevitably lose their jobs." Well, now that women haven't taken off their pants yet, the angry tide of unemployment is already raging like hell. If it really comes to an era when every woman doesn't wear pants, then all the men in the world will surely die clean, but perhaps the world will be at peace then.

Fortunately, the times haven't reached that point yet. Women still wear pants, and men still wear gowns. However, the mysterious relationship between men and women has long disappeared, and what follows is the temptation of flesh. Let's not talk about those "overflowing with fleshy fragrance" and "soul-stirring carnal sensations," but just look at what we see every day, and you will surely believe that I am not mistaken. Don't you see the "agitated X breasts" almost jumping out of the cheongsam, the "swaying X parts" thoroughly arousing the heartstrings, as for those "graceful figures," "slightly exposed jade legs," "blood-red lips," "dark eyelids"... and so on, are just trivial matters.

The giant wheel of the times keeps turning forward, and it cannot be denied that everything is progressing. The mystery between men and women no longer exists, and the status of women has also been raised. Discussions about women's issues are truly the most fashionable thing, especially the debate on women's employment issues, which was heated up once not long ago. Now it's a little quieter, but it doesn't mean the problem has been resolved, it's just that everyone is tired and sits down to take a sip of tea and rest. Although I am a person who prefers mystery, in this era, there is no room for such quirks, but the temptation of flesh is really too excessive, so much so that I am a little frightened. Therefore, I want to advise my fellow women, don't focus solely on rouge and powder, especially those ladies who write about women's issues, before writing articles, be sure not to forget to wipe off the greasepaint on your faces first.

"You are really useless!" Seeing Lian Sun and Gui Sun standing there trembling, knowing that it was also wrong, he shouted, "Pu Ning, pull!" Pu Ning helped Madam up to lean on the chair, while listening to Master's command, he couldn't help but pull the cloth strip. Sixth Master shouted again, "Use force!" and Pu Ning used force. When Madam woke up, she only

saw her son, his eyes bulging out, his tongue hanging out, she was so startled that she cried out and fainted. Sixth Master tested the corpse, it was completely lifeless. He let it fall to the ground, and hurriedly helped Madam, shouting, "Pu Ning, help Madam back." Turning back, he instructed his two good nephews, "Let's go everyone." Lian Sun and Gui Sun each got a revolver hidden away, and followed Sixth Master out of the new house. Sixth Master didn't notice. As soon as Madam entered her own house, she looked up and saw that her son's corpse seemed to be hanging by the bed, she cried out again and fainted. Young Madam came to serve Madam, but she didn't know what was going on. Madam woke up and hugged Young Madam, crying loudly, frantically shouting,

"He, he, followed me into the room!"

"Who, Mother?"

"Didn't you see? He's standing next to you!"

"No one is standing next to me, Mother."

"He's asking for my life, I'll go find his grandfather!"

Madam shouted and was about to get up. Young Madam heard that what she said was wrong, and pressed her down with force. The maid brought ginseng water in to help Young Madam press down on Madam, while comforting Madam to sleep. Madam didn't have much strength either, she drank the ginseng water and slowly fell asleep. Young Madam softly asked the maid,

"Why is Madam like this?"

"I don't know."

From then on, Madam became insane, often shouting,

"He's asking for my life, I'll go find his grandfather!"
