Architectural Supplement

A Glimpse of Ancient Chinese Bridge Architecture (Part 2) 285

— Zhu Zhenmu

(2) Arch Bridges—also known as ring-hole bridges, are a unique style of bridge in China. From an aesthetic point of view, they are extremely beautiful, and from an engineering point of view, they are extremely strong, with a style and structure that reaches perfection. The construction of this type of arch bridge does not use mortar, but is made by stacking stones. The ring-hole is the skeleton of the entire bridge, with low walls on both sides. The space between the two walls is filled with silt and broken bricks, and stone slabs are laid on top, forming steps, which can then become a bridge. Usually, the bridge foundation of an arch bridge is also made of stone blocks or stone strips. The bottom layer must also be densely driven with wooden piles, and stone blocks are densely laid on top of the wooden piles. This is the bridge pier. The bridge pier must be at least one foot above the highest tide level to ensure the safety of the bridge. The stones used to build the low walls must be neat and strong to prevent water leakage. The laying method is the same as laying bricks, with parallel and smooth laying. A stone strip must be laid on the top layer of the wall, with a length that is half the bridge, or two or three strips can be joined together. If the stones used to build the wall are large granite stones, mortar may not be needed. Otherwise, stone seams can be slightly embedded to strengthen and prevent water. After the walls are filled with silt, broken stones, etc., the bridge deck can be laid and stacked into steps. Also, when the low walls are stacked, stone pillars can be erected on both sides near the ring-hole, and a stone strip can be laid across the top of the two opposite pillars to hook and secure them, so as not to deviate. This type of low wall has the function of resisting external forces. The stones of the ring-hole are loosely connected, and when the bridge foundation sinks or is squeezed, they can easily fall off and cause disaster. This type of low wall can prevent problems. However, the low wall cannot resist external bending forces, so the ring-hole must be arched upwards to squeeze against each other. Furthermore, this type of ring-hole is mostly a large arc shape, meaning that the center of the circle is higher than the bridge pier, so the shear force on the two walls is extremely small, making it a very reasonable construction. Sometimes this type of arch bridge experiences tilting due to damage to the bridge foundation and bridge piers. However, if the low walls and ring-hole have not collapsed, they can still be redesigned and remain convenient for traffic, without any drawbacks. This phenomenon can be seen in arch bridges everywhere, which is truly remarkable. The distance between the arch top and the bridge deck has no fixed rule. However, from observation, the larger ones are about one-sixtieth of the span of the arch, and the smaller ones must be within one-thirtieth of the total span, otherwise they will easily be damaged.

(3) Cantilever Bridges—In western and southwestern China, there are very few stone strip bridges, but many cantilever bridges. They are usually built in places where the required bridge span is wide. If the span of the bridge opening is greater than 130 feet, then this type of bridge is necessary. Therefore, wide rivers often use this type of cantilever bridge. The method of construction is to first drive piles and build foundations on both banks, and then use long, large pieces of wood to insert into the foundation, horizontally and diagonally extending outwards, like an arm stretching out. Several layers are extended in this way, and when the distance between the two ends of the top layer is not far, the bridge deck can be laid. This type of bridge deck should be easy to replace, which can save a lot of damage and repair costs. At the joints of the bridge deck on both ends of the cantilever bridge, plywood is used, otherwise it may not be able to bear the weight or there may be danger. The bridge opening of this type of cantilever bridge can also be increased. Simply build another bridge foundation in the river and extend it from both sides, and it can be used.

(4) Suspension Bridges—Suspension bridges are also a unique product of the country's architecture. The raw materials are bamboo bridges and hemp ropes, and their strength and durability are also quite remarkable. They are most often used in places where the river surface is wide and the mountain roads are rugged. They are very easy to see in Sichuan and Yunnan. The method of construction is to erect high frames on both sides of the river or valley and bind them with bamboo ropes. Large baskets are tied on the ropes, which can accommodate about two people, and another thin rope is used to pull them across the river or valley. There is also a simpler method. A high frame is erected on the river bank, and a bamboo rope is tied to it, and this bamboo rope is tied securely to a stone cave at a lower point on the opposite bank. In this way, sliding up and down without pulling the rope can also be used for ferrying; and at the same time, it is installed in reverse in the same way, so it is convenient for both coming and going. Sometimes two parallel bamboo ropes are used to cross a river, with a height difference of five or six feet being appropriate. People can step on the lower rope and hold on to the upper rope with their hands. This is also one type of suspension bridge. Most suspension bridges have one bridge opening. At both ends of the bridge opening, there are station houses, with two pillars in the middle to tie the two ropes, and each is equipped with a windlass to tighten the bamboo ropes, so as not to make them slack. The span of the bridge opening is limited to a maximum of 250 feet. However, there is a suspension bridge on the Min River in Guangxi, which is 700 feet long and 9 feet wide. It is built with ten bamboo ropes with a diameter of 6.5 inches. The structure is divided into six bridge openings, the largest of which spans about 200 feet, and the rest are of varying sizes. There are also as many as five guide ropes. The supports at the most load-bearing parts are made of granite, and the rest are made of wood. The bridge deck is made of ordinary wooden boards, which is extremely safe to walk on, and bamboo pillars and wooden nails are used to strengthen the structure of the bridge body and bridge deck. In addition, metal materials can be said to be absolutely unused, and every year the wooden boards on the bridge deck must be selected and replaced like railway sleepers to avoid danger. The bamboo ropes must also be checked frequently to ensure the safety of travelers. The tensile strength of this type of bamboo suspension bridge is about 26,000 pounds per square inch, so it is extremely load-bearing. Its origin is said to be in Tibet, because even today, this type of bridge is most often built in Tibet.

In addition to bamboo, suspension bridges can also be made of iron chains. However, this only appeared after the 15th century and is an advancement of bamboo bridges. The method is still the same as described above and does not need to be described separately.

In summary, China's achievements in bridge construction can be seen from the above, and the popularity of bridges is even more astonishing. There are currently no statistics on the total number of bridges in the country. However, according to Marco Polo's records when he visited Hangzhou, there were more than 1,200 bridges of all sizes in Hangzhou at that time (13th century). Therefore, including all 30 provinces and urban areas in the country, there should be no fewer than 5 million bridges.

A Humble Suggestion for the Construction of Common Public Buildings 286

— Qin

(1) Introduction

The construction of public buildings (or simply apartments) has been extremely developed in Shanghai in recent years. The tall buildings of seven or eight stories, soaring into the clouds, can be said to be solemn and magnificent, economical and practical. In Shanghai, where land is worth its weight in gold, this is indeed worthy of our attention and study. However, the current construction of such apartments mostly tends to be luxurious, with too much emphasis on decoration. It seems that the purpose is not at all to pay attention to the housing problems of ordinary city residents, but rather to compete and strive for height, which inevitably violates the principle. Therefore, the construction cost is very large. Instead of seeking innovation and research in materials, the focus is on magnificent appearance, so those who enter and exit are bound to be big bosses of foreign firms and managers of companies. The monthly rent is hundreds of dollars. They drive their own cars every day, leisurely and comfortably. This kind of good fortune can only be enjoyed by the rich, and even more often by foreigners. Very few Chinese people can enjoy it. Can we say that this phenomenon is the development of social economy and the trend of new life for the people? No, this is just a kind of equipment for the enjoyment of the rich. It is of no benefit to ordinary residents. Then why can't we use this good construction method, apply the progress of modern civilization, to make the housing of our general residents get safe and comfortable new equipment? To make the benefits of construction reach the general residents, the only way is to make it popular. This is not to say simple or sloppy, but just to think of ways to reduce the cost of construction, so the rent can be suitable for the living standards of ordinary residents.

(2) Benefits of Apartments

The construction of apartments is very developed in foreign countries, but in China, it has only gradually risen in recent years. The trend has a vigorous atmosphere. However, the disadvantage is that it cannot be popular and cannot fully express its benefits. As for our current residential buildings, they are specially equipped for one family to live in. They take up space, cost a lot of money, and are very uneconomical. Like in the alleys, several families have to live in one house, which is as narrow as a pigeon coop. Simplicity and sloppiness need not be said. No attention is paid to hygiene, nor is cleanliness sought. The avoidance of fire is not considered at all. Promote the general industry and commerce of architecture

(3) Construction of Apartments

The construction of popular apartments cannot be sloppy, and the equipment cannot be simplified, but magnificence is not necessary, and decoration is not necessary. I think that popular apartments should have the following conditions, which are:

(1) Safety, such as the firmness of the building and the avoidance of fire;

(2) Cleanliness, because neatness is beauty, and cleanliness can prevent epidemics;

(3) Comfort, living must be comfortable, but not luxury, because luxury is too uneconomical, and it is not necessarily comfortable; (4) Grandeur, grandeur is not in the emphasis on decoration, but the overall appearance of the building, majestic and grand.

These four conditions of safety, cleanliness, comfort, and grandeur should not only be paid attention to when building apartments, but also all buildings cannot be separated from these conditions. However, the construction of apartments has a great limitation, that is, the construction cost should be saved as much as possible. Then, for this kind of building, we must not follow the old habits, and we must conduct a lot of research and consideration on the materials. The construction of wood is not durable, which is a great disadvantage, and it is easy to cause fire. The construction of steel is not cheap at present. If we can use steel units to build houses in the future, then the materials can be produced in large quantities, and the price will naturally be much cheaper. There is also a method of constructing concrete, which is relatively suitable and uses various concrete building units. It is both strong and cheap to build. This construction method is very worthy of our research. As for the construction method, it is originally changing with each passing day. Of course, there is no need to stick to one method, nor is it necessary to copy other people's inventions. We must strive for improvement and surpass others. This is what architects and engineers should strive for. What we have at hand now are scientific theories and mechanical inventions. If we want to research, if we want to experiment, if we want to create, what is so difficult about this!

The various equipment in the apartment should be as scientific as possible, and the interests of the public should be taken into account, such as the heating equipment of the house, the ventilation equipment, the adjustment of air, the installation of windows, and even the supply of electricity and tap water, etc., should all strive for new styles, reduce costs, and enable residents to enjoy great benefits, while only bearing limited and light expenses. How can we achieve this level? Only by applying science as much as possible, and when it comes to the issue of management, that is also very important. Otherwise, even if there is good equipment, it cannot be guaranteed for a long time. If there is a machine with high efficiency, it cannot be used well. Isn't it a pity? Inefficiency is a natural result, which is to make residents bear more burden on the apartment. The principle is not in line.

Special attention should be paid to the prevention of diseases in the apartment, because there are many residents in the apartment, and it is very easy to spread. Therefore, cleanliness is extremely important. The introduction of sunlight and the circulation of air are especially important in places with many people. It is best to have open spaces around the apartment, plant trees, so that children can play, and adults can rest, which is beneficial to hygiene and beauty.

(4) Apartments and the Prosperity of the City

Shanghai can be considered prosperous. The population is more than 3 million. The development of commerce is the first in the country and world-renowned. Everything is inferior to that of other parts of the country. Therefore, those who are responsible for public security feel that their duties are very important. Not only must they maintain the current prosperity of Shanghai, but they must also plan for new developments in the future. Mr. Sun Yat-sen was the first to discover the shortcomings of Shanghai's business circle. Therefore, we now have the plan for this Greater Shanghai. However, the more developed a city is, the more people there will be, and the problem of accommodation becomes a very important problem. Therefore, I think the construction of apartments is very worthy of research. If we say that all the residences in Shanghai are apartment-style, then the population can definitely be increased by ten times, twenty times, or even dozens of times on the same foundation. In total, it is not difficult for the population of Shanghai to increase to 10 million. As the population increases, commerce will become more and more developed, and the prosperity of the city will be rising steadily. Who can predict the bright future with numbers? Keys Dowdeswells well designed

The municipal houses on Meibake Road, Qingdao Road and Pike Road cover an area of ​​24 mu. Architect Kai is a member of the Royal Institute of British Architects. There are countless tall buildings designed in Singapore. Now he has an office in Hamilton Building on Jiangxi Road. The new house that our library is currently adding is also designed by Mr. Kai.

Domestic Stone Materials Suitable for Construction 288

— Dawei

During my spring break, I traveled to Beijing. After enjoying the famous scenic spots, I traveled all over the city streets. The public works and hygiene are cleaner than before, but the commercial progress seems to be slow. Although the buildings, such as railway transportation departments, are beautified by combining Chinese and Western styles, they do not lose the inherent essence of the East, but this is not surprising. What is most noteworthy is the facade of the Juxingcheng Bank in Xinjiekou. Observing the stone materials, the black ones are like granite and strong, and the green ones are like marble and solid. They are bright enough to be used as mirrors, and they shine with the sunlight. Those who pass by stop and watch, sighing that they are rare. I was also curious and wanted to find out which country produced them. I have heard that the black stone of this benefit and the green flower stone of Italy have long been famous in the world, and they seem to be close to them. I dare not despise domestic products, but I have never thought that China could have such great achievements. Later, I was told by the craftsmen that they were indeed pure Chinese stone materials, produced near Laoshan Mountain in Qingdao, and constructed by the Chinese Stone Company. I asked where the Chinese Stone Company was located, and why had I never heard of it. The craftsman replied that it was in Qingdao, and that there was also a branch in Shanghai. I was very happy to hear this, and lingered to watch and study again. It is a pity that they were used sparingly. If large buildings were used, wouldn't it be magnificent? After returning to Shanghai, I went to the company at No. 33 Sichuan Road to visit. There were many kinds of stones, colorful and beautiful. I learned that the black stone was called feldspar, and the green flower was called jade Buddha stone. Compared with the quality of black and Italian green, they are not as good. China has hidden rare goods for a long time, and it does not know how to use them. Instead, it relies on foreigners. Stones are like this, let alone other things? The company that created this initiative is also great. I hope that it will move forward bravely and take the lead in the world of stone materials. This is a matter of course. As the saying goes, "Although the peony is good, it needs green leaves to support it." It also depends on the architects to use it more, so that domestic products can be promoted and foreign goods can be prevented in case. This is a great pleasure during my trip to Nanjing. I write it down and want to introduce it to all walks of life.
